GSUM DANG, LAM GYI NGO BO LA RMONGS PA SGRIB PA THAMS CAD ZHI BA'I
LAM LA RMONGS PA DANG, LAM GYI DMIGS PA LA RMONGS PA DE BZHIN NYID
LA SOGS PA DANG, GZUGS

SOGS MTSUNGS PAR LDAN PA BDEN GNYIS NGO BO GCIG PA DANG MI LDAN
PA, BDEN GNYIS NGO BO THA DAD PA LA RMONGS PA DANG, THEG DMAN
DANG THEG CHEN GYI LAM MI MNYAM PA LA RMONGS PA DANG, SDUG
BSNGAL LA SOGS PA'I CHOS NYID LA RMONGS PA

GYI

THA MAR BZHED PA'I PHYIR,
